-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 **How long have you been working remotely?**
  - Less than 1 month
  - 1-6 months
  - 6-12 months
  - More than 1 year

**What is your role in the company?**
  - Executive/Senior Management
  - Manager
  - Staff/Employee

**Do you feel that you have the necessary resources and tools to effectively work remotely?**
  - Yes
  - No
  - Not sure

**How would you rate the communication and collaboration with your team while working remotely?**
  - Very good
  - Somewhat good
  - Neutral
  - Somewhat bad
  - Very bad

**Do you feel that your productivity has increased or decreased since you started working remotely?**
  - Increased
  - Decreased
  - Not sure

**How would you rate the support you have received from the company in terms of transitioning to remote work?**
  - Very good
  - Somewhat good
  - Neutral
  - Somewhat bad
  - Very bad

**What is your preferred method of communication when working remotely?**
  - Email
  - Phone
  - Video calls
  - Chat/Messaging
  - Other

**Do you feel that your remote working location is conducive to productivity?**
  - Yes
  - No

**Feedback Mechanisms**

**Importance of Feedback**

* How important do you consider feedback in a workplace setting?
* On a scale of 1-10, how would you rate the importance of feedback?

**Feedback Types**

* Which type of feedback do you prefer: positive or negative?
* Do you think that constructive criticism is more effective than direct negative feedback?

**Feedback Frequency**

* How often do you like to give and receive feedback?
* Is there a specific frequency that you think is ideal?

**Feedback Receiver**

* Who do you prefer to give feedback to: your manager, colleagues, or subordinates?
* Is it easier to give feedback to someone who is not in your team?

**Feedback Medium**

* Which medium do you prefer to use when giving feedback: in-person, video call, or email?
* Is there a specific medium that you think is more effective than others?

**Feedback Barriers**

* What barriers do you think prevent people from giving feedback?
* Do you think that people are more likely to give feedback if they are anonymous?

**Feedback and Personal Growth**

* How does feedback affect your personal growth and development?
* Is it easier to accept feedback that can help you grow as a person?

This JSON object represents a questionnaire for evaluating the health and safety measures of a company. The questionnaire consists of 7 questions, each with a unique code, name, and type. The type of each question is specified using the type\_ID field, and the display order is used to order the questions. The answers to each question are also specified using the\_TF\_ANSWERS field. The answers are represented as a list of strings, and the order in which they appear in this list determines the order in which they will be displayed to the user. The answers are also associated with a unique code that can be used to identify them. The questionnaire can be used to collect feedback about the health and safety measures of a company and evaluate their effectiveness.

 **Do you think that the company has an effective health and safety program in place?**

  - No
  - Partially

  - No
  - Sometimes

  - Occasionally
  - Rarely
  - Never

**Do you feel that the company provides adequate resources to maintain a safe and healthy work environment?**

  - No
  - Partially

**Have you ever felt at risk while performing your job due to inadequate health and safety measures?**

  - No
  - Sometimes

    - Neutral
